<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:voorkomen.html>voorkomen</a> (1776)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

</p>
<ol><li>to exist, to occur
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>Deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:soort.html>soort</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:komt.html>komt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a></b> in <a href = vnd.unilang:afrika.html>Afrika</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>This species doesn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <b>occur</b> in Africa.</dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aarde.html>Aarde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zover.html>zover</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bekend.html>bekend</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:enige.html>enige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:plek.html>plek</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heelal.html>heelal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>waar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:leven.html>leven</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:voorkomt.html>voorkomt</a></b> of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gekomen.html>gekomen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:woonplaats.html>woonplaats</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:miljoenen.html>miljoenen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:soorten.html>soorten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:organismen.html>organismen</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>The Earth <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>, as far as it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> known, the only place in the universe where life <b>occurs</b> or <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <b>occurred</b> and <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the habitat of millions of species of organisms.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>to happen

<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">before, in front of</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voorman.html>voorman</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voormannen.html>voormannen</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">voorlieden</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voorman.html>voormannetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<ol><li>supervisor, <a href = vnd.unilang:foreman.html>foreman</a>, ganger</li>

***voornaamwoord.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:voornaamwoord.html>voornaamwoord</a> (86373)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">for</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:naam.html>naam</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">name, noun</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:woord.html>woord</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">word</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">prōnōmen</i> with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:woord.html>woord</a></i> added to disambiguate it from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voornaam.html>voornaam</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">first name, given name</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

</p>

***voorstellen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:voorstellen.html>voorstellen</a> (884)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vorestellen</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stellen.html>stellen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voorstellen.html>voorstellen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to present, to put forth, to introduce</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to propose, to suggest
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schaal.html>Schaal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Kardasjev <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:russische.html>Russische</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:astronoom.html>astronoom</a> Nikolaj Kardasjev <b>voorgestelde</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:indeling.html>indeling</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:technologische.html>technologische</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ontwikkeling.html>ontwikkeling</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beschavingen.html>beschavingen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The Kardashev scale <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a system <b>proposed</b> by the Russian astronomer Nicolai Kardashev for classifying the technological development of civilizations.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to imagine
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:stel.html>Stel</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:landen.html>landen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Imagine</b> there's no countries.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>

<p>From Middle Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">voreteken</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">portent</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from Old Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">furitekan</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">before</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teken.html>teken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sign</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
